     $('.hamburger').on('click',function(e){
        e.stopPropagation();
          $('.m-header').removeClass('index');
        if($(this).hasClass('on')){
            $(this).removeClass('on');
            $('.m-nav').stop().slideUp();
            changeHeader()
            // onTouchMove(false);
            $('body').css("top", "").removeClass('no-scroll');
            $(window).scrollTop(bodyScroll);
        }else{
            $(this).addClass('on');
            $('.m-nav').stop().slideDown();
            bodyScroll=window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop || document.body.scrollTop || 0;
            $('body').addClass('no-scroll').css({top : -bodyScroll});

        }
    });
    $('.m-nav li .tit').on('click',function(e){
        e.stopPropagation();
        var _this = $(this);
        var thisLi = _this.parent();
        if(thisLi.hasClass('on')){
            thisLi.removeClass('on');
            _this.next().stop().slideUp();
        }else{
            thisLi.addClass('on').siblings().removeClass('on');
            $('.m-nav li .navson').stop().slideUp();
            _this.next().stop().slideDown();
        }
    })
    $('.m-nav .lis .tits').on('click',function(e){
        e.stopPropagation();
        var _this = $(this);
        var thisLi = _this.parent();
        if(thisLi.hasClass('on')){
            thisLi.removeClass('on');
            _this.next().stop().slideUp();
        }else{
            thisLi.addClass('on').siblings().removeClass('on');
            $('.m-nav li .navson_son').stop().slideUp();
            _this.next().stop().slideDown();
        }
    })
    $(".main_nav .right .box").click(function(){
        if($(this).hasClass("on")){
            $(this).removeClass("on")
            $(".main_nav .right form").fadeOut("400")
        }else{
          $(this).addClass("on")
          $(".main_nav .right form").fadeIn("400")
        }
        
    })
    function gosubmit(){
        $(".headersub").click()
    }

</script>

<div class="tit-84 col-fff text-uppercase hnb lh1">AI-POET <span class="rdw">TM</span></div>
<div class="indexline"></div>
<div class="con">
<div class="tit-50 col-fff hnr">5T Connection for an Intelligent Era</div>
<div class="tit-18 col-fff hnr">AI-POET<span class="rdw" style="font-size: 12px;">TM</span> is our core strategy intergrating the 5 core technologies of PT (Process Technology) and ET (Equipment Technology), OT (Operational Technology), AT (Automation Technology), IT (Information Technology). By leveraging our expertise in process industry, we help booster process industry to achieve high quality, green, and sustainable development.</div>

					    var delta = (event.originalEvent.wheelDelta && (event.originalEvent.wheelDelta > 0 ? 1 : -1)) || 
					                (event.originalEvent.detail && (event.originalEvent.detail > 0 ? -1 : 1));
					    console.log(delta)
					    if (delta < 0 && flag) {
					    	flag = false;
					    	// $("html").css({
			       //  			overflow: 'hidden',
				      //   		"overflow-y": "scroll",
				      //   	});
						      // var top5 = $(".index_con").offset().top-68
					       //  	$('html, body').stop().animate({
							     //    scrollTop: top5
							     // }, 1000);
						    }
						}
					});
               
                
		        	 
		        	
        }
        function removeActive(el){
                $(el).removeClass('active')
                $(".tec_cont").removeClass('slcol')
               
        }
        $(".home_e .table ").on('click', 'a', function(event) {
					event.preventDefault();
					$(this).addClass('on').siblings().removeClass('on')
					var type = $(this).attr("data_type")
					 var newUrl = "https://en.supcon.com/ajax/indexnews.html"
		        	$.ajax({
			            url: newUrl,
			            data: {type: type},
			            success:function(data){
			                      $(".index_ajax").html(data)
			                      $(".news-container").addClass('show')
			            }
	        		})
		});
		$(".home_e .table ").on('mouseenter', 'a', function(event) {
					event.preventDefault();
					$(this).addClass('on').siblings().removeClass('on')
					var type = $(this).attr("data_type")
					 var newUrl = "https://en.supcon.com/ajax/indexnews.html"
		        	$.ajax({
			            url: newUrl,
			            data: {type: type},
			            success:function(data){
			                      $(".index_ajax").html(data)
			                      $(".news-container").addClass('show')
			            }
	        		})
		});
         $(".home_e .table a").eq(0).click()

			    slidesPerView : "auto",

         var suptimer1 = null
          var suptimer2 = null
         	function addsupActive(el){
         		$("html").css({
		        		overflow: 'hidden',
		        	});
           	$("#overlay").addClass('on')
           	suptimer1 = setTimeout(function() {
		        	 		$("#overlay").addClass('big')
		        	 }, 800 )
           	suptimer2 = setTimeout(function() {

		        	 		addClassActive(".tec")
		        	 },1800 )
           	
           }
           function removesupActive(el){
           	removeClassActive(".tec")
           	$("#overlay").removeClass('big')
           	$("#overlay").removeClass('on')
           	clearTimeout(suptimer1 )
           	clearTimeout(suptimer2 )
           	$("html").css({
			        		overflow: 'hidden',
			        		"overflow-y": "scroll",
			 });
           }
    </script>
